11 Section 2. R.S. 6:333(F)(14) is hereby amended and reenacted to read as follows:
12 §333. Disclosure of financial records; reimbursement of costs
13 * * *
14 F. The following disclosures by a bank or any affiliate are hereby specifically
15 authorized and, except as otherwise provided in this Subsection, nothing in this
16 Section shall prohibit, restrict, or otherwise apply to:
17 * * *
18 (14) The disclosure by a bank or any affiliate of data match information on
19 an individual to the attorney general secretary of the Department of Children and
20 Family Services, or his designee in the office of children and family services, child
21 support enforcement section, for use in attempting to establish, modify, or enforce
22 a child support obligation of such individual. Such disclosure to the department shall
23 be limited to the name, record address, social security or taxpayer identification
24 number, and an average daily account balance for the most recent thirty-day period,
25 of a noncustodial parent who maintains an account at such institution and who owes
26 past-due support as identified by the state by name and social security or taxpayer
27 identification number. The disclosure authorization provided for in this Paragraph
28 shall apply to all co-owners listed on the applicable account.
29 * * *

36 §58. Definitions

38 * * *
39 (4) "Domestic violence shelter" means a community-based shelter for victims

43 §252. Duplicate records of marriage licenses issued; preservation; filing of duplicate
44 copy with state division of vital records; penalty for failure to file
45 * * *
46 C. The other copy shall be filed with the division of vital records of the
47 Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services Health and Human
48 Services within ten days of the expiration of each month, and the failure, neglect, or
49 refusal to do so shall be punished by a fine of not less than ten dollars nor more than
50 fifty dollars.
51 * * *
52 §254. Penalty for failure to file or complete marriage certificate
53 Any person authorized to perform marriages in this state who fails to
54 complete the forms provided by the Louisiana Department of Children and Family
55 Services Health and Human Services, and specifically fails to fill in the date and
56 place the ceremony was performed, or neglects or fails to file the two executed
57 copies with the clerk of court in the parish where the license was issued or, if in
58 Orleans Parish, with the state office of vital records, within ten days after the date of
59 the marriage as provided by law, shall be fined not less than twenty dollars for the
60 first offense, fifty dollars for the second offense, and one hundred dollars for a third
Page 3 of 111

1 offense, and the offender shall be prohibited thereafter from officiating at any
2 marriage in this state.

4 §303. Income assignment; new orders; deviation
5 A. In all new child support orders after January 1, 1994, that are not being
6 enforced by the Department of Children and Family Services Justice, the court shall
7 include as part of the order an immediate income assignment unless there is a written
8 agreement between the parties or the court finds good cause not to require an
9 immediate income assignment.
10 * * *
11 §311. Modification or suspension of support; material change in circumstances;
12 periodic review by Department of Children and Family Services
13 Justice; medical support
14 A.
15 * * *
16 (2) The Department of Children and Family Services Justice shall prepare
17 and distribute information, forms, and rules for the modification or suspension of
18 support orders, in accordance with this Subsection, and for proceeding in forma
19 pauperis. The information provided by the Department of Children and Family
20 Services Justice shall specifically include what may constitute a material change in
21 circumstances. The clerks of court in all parishes shall make this information
22 available to the public upon request. This information shall also be distributed by the
23 Department of Public Safety and Corrections or the sheriff of any parish, as
24 appropriate, to every person incarcerated in every state and parish jail and prison
25 facility. When the initial support order is entered, either the court or the department,
26 if providing services, shall provide this information to the parties.
27 * * *
28 C. For purposes of this Section, in cases where the Department of Children
29 and Family Services Justice is providing support enforcement services:
30 * * *
31 §311.1. Child support during the obligor's incarceration; Department of Children
32 and Family Services Justice providing support enforcement services
33 * * *
34 C. The Department of Public Safety and Corrections or the sheriff of any
35 parish, as appropriate, shall notify the Department of Children and Family Services
36 Justice of any person who has been in their custody and may be subject to a child
37 support order if either:
38 * * *

40 Subsection is scheduled to be released from incarceration. The timeframe for such
41 notification under this Paragraph shall be determined by an interagency agreement
42 between the Department of Children and Family Services Justice and the
43 Department of Public Safety and Corrections.
44 D. When the Department of Children and Family Services Justice is
45 providing support enforcement services, the department shall, upon receipt of notice
46 in accordance with Subsection C of this Section, provide notice to the custodial party
47 by regular mail.
48 * * *
49 G.
50 * * *
51 (3)(a)(i) If the obligor is released from incarceration while the child is a
52 minor, the Department of Children and Family Services Justice or either party shall
53 petition the court prior to the first day of the second full month after the obligor's
54 release from incarceration for a modification hearing to establish the terms of the
55 previously suspended child support order. Unless the terms of the order of support
56 have been otherwise modified, the suspended order of support shall resume at the
57 same terms that existed before the suspension.

6 §396. Authority for test; ex parte orders; use of results
7 * * *
8 B.(1) The district attorney, in assisting the Department of Children and
9 Family Services Justice in establishing paternity as authorized by R.S. 46:236.1.1
10 et seq., may file a motion with a court of proper jurisdiction and venue prior to and
11 without the necessity of filing any other legal proceeding. Upon ex parte motion of
12 the district attorney and sworn affidavit of the party alleging specific facts tending
13 to prove paternity and other facts necessary to establish the jurisdiction and venue
14 of the court, the court shall issue an ex parte order directing the mother, her husband
15 or former husband, child, and alleged father to appear at a certain date and time to
16 submit to the collection of blood or tissue samples, or both, and shall direct that
17 inherited characteristics in the samples, including but not limited to blood and tissue
18 type, be determined by appropriate testing procedures. The order shall be personally
19 served upon the alleged father. If any party refuses to submit to such tests, the court,
20 in a subsequent civil action in which paternity is a relevant fact, may resolve the
21 question of paternity against such party or enforce its order if the rights of others and
22 the interests of justice so require.
23 * * *
24 §399.1. Dismissal of final order following judgment of paternity; time periods;
25 procedure; effects
26 A. Notwithstanding any other provision of law, a judgment establishing
27 paternity may be set aside or vacated by the adjudicated father of a child, the child,
28 the mother of the child, or the legal representative of any of these persons. The
29 proceeding shall be instituted by ordinary process in a court of competent
30 jurisdiction and service shall be made upon the office of children and family
31 services, child support enforcement section of the Department of Children and
32 Family Services, the Department of Justice if services are being provided by the
33 department. The burden of proof shall be upon the party seeking to set aside or
34 vacate the judgment of paternity. The proceeding shall be brought within a two-year
35 period commencing with the date on which the adjudicated father knew or should
36 have known of a judgment that established him as the father of the child or
37 commencing with the date the adjudicated father knew or should have known of the
38 existence of an action to adjudicate the issue of paternity, whichever is first.
39 * * *
40 F.
41 * * *
42 (3) The judgment dismissing an established order of support shall be served
43 upon the office of children and family services, child support enforcement section
44 of the Department of Children and Family Services, Department of Justice if
45 services are being provided by the department.
46 (4) Neither the state of Louisiana, its officers, employees, agents, contractors,
47 nor the office of children and family services, child support enforcement section of
48 the Department of Children and Family Services Department of Justice shall be
49 liable in any case to compensate any person for child support paid or for any other
50 costs as a result of the judgment setting aside or vacating the judgment of paternity
51 or support entered in accordance with this Section.
52 * * *
53 §404. Father's paternity action; time period; exception
54 The peremptive periods in Civil Code Article 198 shall apply to the
55 Department of Children and Family Services Justice when providing services in
56 accordance with 42 USC 666.

61 §3881. General exemptions from seizure
Page 9 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 A. The following income or property of a debtor is exempt from seizure
2 under any writ, mandate, or process whatsoever, except as otherwise herein
3 provided:
4 (1)(a) Seventy-five percent of his disposable earnings for any week, but in
5 no case shall this exemption be less than an amount in disposable earnings which is
6 equal to thirty times the federal minimum hourly wage in effect at the time the
7 earnings are payable or a multiple or fraction thereof, according to whether the
8 employee's pay period is greater or less than one week. However, the exemption
9 from disposable earnings for the payment of a current or past due support obligation,
10 or both, for a child or children is fifty percent of disposable earnings, and the
11 exemption from seizure of the disposable earnings for the payment of a current or
12 past due support obligation, or both, for a spouse or former spouse is sixty percent
13 of the disposable earnings. For purposes of this Subsection, if the Department of
14 Children and Family Services Justice is providing support enforcement services to
15 the spouse and a judgment or order for support includes an obligation for both a child
16 or children and a spouse or former spouse, or in any case wherein the judgment or
17 order does not clearly indicate which amount is attributable to support of the child
18 or children and which amount is attributable to support of the spouse or former
19 spouse, the support obligation shall be treated as if it is exclusively for the support
20 of a child or children.
21 * * *
22 §3928. Priority of judgment, decree, or order of support
23 In any criminal or civil matter, a judgment, decree, order, or sentence of
24 court, or a sale, transfer, or assignment of earnings by which a person is obligated to
25 pay for the current or past due support, or both, of a child or children, or of a parent
26 of a child or children if the Department of Children and Family Services Justice is
27 providing support enforcement services to the parent, shall prime in enforcement any
28 prior or subsequent judgment, decree, order, or sentence of court, or sale, transfer,
29 or assignment of earnings, and shall be satisfied out of the nonexempt portion of
30 disposable earnings.
31 * * *
32 §4291. Effect of child support payments; judicial mortgage and privilege; affidavit
33 of support owed; prescription
34 B.(1) In all cases where the Department of Children and Family Services
35 Justice is enforcing child support services, a judgment created by operation of law
36 pursuant to Subsection A of this Section shall be executory in all respects, without
37 the necessity of a judicial proceeding to determine the amount actually owed. The
38 director of the child support enforcement section, office of children and family
39 services, Department of Children and Family Services attorney general, or his
40 designee shall certify the actual amount in an affidavit entitled "Child Support
41 Mortgage and Privilege by Affidavit of DCFS". Such affidavit shall have the effect
42 of a judgment. Notwithstanding any other law to the contrary, prescription shall not
43 begin to run against any such judgment until the child reaches the age of majority or
44 the obligation to provide child support ceases.
45 * * *
46 C. The department shall provide notice by certified mail, by personal service,
47 or by domiciliary service, to the child support obligor thirty days prior to a "Child
48 Support Mortgage and Privilege by Affidavit of DCFS" being filed and recorded.
49 The notice shall advise the child support obligor that he has fifteen days to file an
50 appeal. Upon notice of appeal, the department shall schedule a judicial hearing.
51 Notwithstanding any other law to the contrary, prescription shall not begin to run
52 against any such judgment until the child reaches the age of majority or the
53 obligation to provide child support ceases.

50 1353, the judge may suspend the execution or imposition of sentence and release the

54 sentence imposed and may impose any specific conditions reasonably related to the

56 set forth in Code of Criminal Procedure Article 895.

8 defined in 42 U.S.C. 672, licensed by the department, shall request in writing that the
9 bureau supply information to ascertain whether that person or persons have been
10 arrested for or convicted of, or pled nolo contendere to, any criminal offense. The
11 request must be on a form prepared by the bureau and signed by a responsible officer
12 or official of the organization or department making the request. It must include a
13 statement signed by the person about whom the request is made which gives his
14 permission for such information to be released.

33 §934. Detention centers
34 A. All facilities that detain juveniles pursuant to Title VII or Title VIII of the
35 Louisiana Children's Code shall collect and maintain data on each child detained.
36 This data shall be retained permanently by the facility and shall be made available
37 for inspection during normal business hours by any court exercising juvenile court
38 jurisdiction, by the Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services Health
39 and Human Services, and by persons collecting aggregate statistical information.

48 §1081. Purpose
49 Notwithstanding any other provision of law to the contrary, the provisions of
50 this Part shall serve as the sole statutory authorization under which the Department
51 of Children and Family Services or Louisiana Department of Health and Human
52 Services and the Department of Public Safety and Corrections shall make payments
53 for the care and treatment of children in nonstate operated child caring agencies,
54 child placing agencies, shelter care facilities, and maternity homes.
55 * * *
56 §1083. Participation
57 Nonstate operated agencies and facilities desiring to participate in payment
58 under this Part shall:
59 (1) If otherwise required by statute or regulation, be duly licensed by the state
60 of Louisiana through its agent, the Department of Children and Family Services or
61 Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services.
Page 15 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 (2) Submit to the Department of Children and Family Services or Louisiana
2 Department of Health and Human Services or the Department of Public Safety and
3 Corrections on or before August first, or at a time set by the department, a statement
4 requesting participation and funding under this Part for the succeeding fiscal year.
5 (3) Submit programmatic and fiscal information within such time and to the
6 extent as the Department of Children and Family Services or Louisiana Department
7 of Health and Human Services or the Department of Public Safety and Corrections
8 may require. Agencies or facilities which operate multiple subprograms shall submit
9 such information for each subprogram for which participation is being requested.
10 The failure of an agency or facility to submit such a statement or to provide
11 information required by these departments may, at their discretion, preclude that
12 agency or facility from participating in funding under this Part for the fiscal year in
13 question.
14 (4) Be subject to audit by the Department of Children and Family Services
15 or Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services or the Department of
16 Public Safety and Corrections and the legislative auditor, and shall retain and make
17 available such records and documents as are required to complete such audit.
18 §1084. Establishment of rates for payment for care in nonstate operated agencies
19 and facilities
20 A. For purposes of establishing rates of payment the Department of Children
21 and Family Services or Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services and
22 the Department of Public Safety and Corrections shall develop a formula that bears
23 a reasonable relationship to cost of care for children cared for by nonstate operated
24 institutions and agencies and which incorporates a prospective budgeting
25 methodology. For purposes of establishing such rates each department named herein
26 shall develop criteria for budgeting that reflect established accounting practices and
27 encourage cost containment.
28 B. On the basis of information provided in accordance with R.S. 15:1083, the
29 Department of Children and Family Services or Louisiana Department of Health and
30 Human Services and the Department of Public Safety and Corrections shall pay
31 monthly to each nonstate operated institution or agency a sum computed by these
32 departments using a formula that bears a reasonable relationship to cost of care for
33 children cared for by the nonstate operated institutions and agencies and which
34 incorporates a prospective budgeting methodology.
35 C. The Department of Children and Family Services or Louisiana Department
36 of Health and Human Services and the Department of Public Safety and
37 Corrections may make revisions to these rates provided that all of the following
38 conditions are met:
39 (1) The Department of Children and Family Services or Louisiana
40 Department of Health and Human Services or the Department of Public Safety and
41 Corrections submits a report to the legislature documenting the need for such
42 revisions.
43 * * *
44 D. The Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services, Department
45 of Children and Family Services and the Department of Public Safety and
46 Corrections shall promulgate under the Administrative Procedure Act and publish
47 in the Louisiana Register the criteria utilized in establishing the cost related formula
48 that bears a reasonable relationship to cost of care for children cared for by nonstate
49 operated institutions and agencies. Each department may set its own rates and make
50 payment based on that rate.
51 §1085. Payment for care and treatment
52 A. The Department of Children and Family Services or Louisiana
53 Department of Health and Human Services is hereby authorized to make payments,
54 at the rates established under R.S. 15:1084, for the care and treatment of children
55 placed by the Department of Children and Family Services or Louisiana Department
56 of Health and Human Services in child caring agencies, child placing agencies,
57 maternity homes, and shelter care facilities which conform to the requirements of
58 this Part.
59 B. Payments shall be made on a monthly basis and shall represent
60 reimbursements for services provided during the previous month. Participating
61 agencies shall submit such information as the Department of Children and Family
Page 16 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 Services or Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services may require to
2 document claims for reimbursement.
3 C. Participating agencies and facilities shall receive one and only one
4 monthly payment from the Department of Children and Family Services or Louisiana
5 Department of Health and Human Services for services rendered to each child
6 under this Part except for such adjustments as may be necessary to rectify previous
7 inaccurate payments.
8 * * *
9 §1086. Contribution to cost of care by parent, custodian
10 A. When the Department of Children and Family Services or Louisiana
11 Department of Health and Human Services or the Department of Public Safety and
12 Corrections provides payments for care and treatment of a child under the provisions
13 of this Part, the parent or legal custodian will be required to contribute to the cost of
14 care of the child in such a manner as is consistent with applicable federal and state
15 regulations, as is commensurate with his ability to pay, and as is in accordance with
16 a sliding scale which shall be established by the departments.

44 §192.1. Meals; denial to students; procedures
45 A. If the governing authority of a public elementary school, for any reason,
46 adopts a policy of denying a scheduled meal to a child who is an elementary school
47 student, it shall implement the following procedures to provide for safeguards to the
48 child's health and the child's ability to learn:
49 (1) Prior to withholding a meal from the child, the school shall do each of the
50 following:
51 (a) Provide actual notification to the child's parent or legal guardian as to the
52 date and time after which meals may be denied, the reason for such denial, any
53 action that may be taken by the parent or legal guardian to prevent further denial of
54 meals, and the consequences of the failure to take appropriate actions to prevent such
55 denial, including that the school governing authority shall contact the office of
56 children and family services within child welfare, the Louisiana Department of
57 Children and Family Services Health and Human Services upon the third instance
58 of such denial during a single school year as provided in Paragraph (3) of this
59 Subsection.
60 * * *
61 (3) Upon the third instance during a single school year of the same
62 elementary school child being denied a meal during school hours, the school
Page 18 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 governing authority shall contact the office of children and family services within
2 child welfare, the Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services Health
3 and Human Services to report the failure of the parent or guardian to pay for meals
4 which has resulted in repeated denials of meals during school hours.
5 * * *
6 C. If the governing authority of a public elementary school adopts a policy
7 of denying a scheduled meal to a child, the governing authority shall document each
8 instance that a child is denied a meal in the elementary school under its authority.
9 Such documentation shall be provided upon request to the state superintendent of
10 education, to the secretary of the Louisiana Department of Children and Family
11 Services Health and Human Services, the House Committee on Education, or the
12 Senate Committee on Education.
13 * * *
14 §238. Education of children having no permanent address, certain abandoned
15 children, and children in foster care
16 A. Notwithstanding any provision of law or regulation to the contrary, the
17 governing authority of each public elementary and secondary school shall establish
18 a policy to provide for the placement in school and for the education of any child
19 temporarily residing within the jurisdiction of the board who has no permanent
20 address, who has been abandoned by his parents, or who is in foster care pursuant
21 to placement through the Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services
22 Health and Human Services.
23 B. No governing authority of a public elementary or secondary school shall
24 deny enrollment in school to any child solely because the child has no permanent
25 address, because the child has been abandoned by his parents, or because the child
26 is in foster care pursuant to placement through the Louisiana Department of
27 Children and Family Services Health and Human Services; however, nothing in
28 this Section shall require the enrollment of any child not permitted by another school
29 system to attend school, either permanently or temporarily, as a result of disciplinary
30 actions.
31 C. The governing authority of each public elementary and secondary school
32 shall establish a policy to ensure that a child who is in foster care pursuant to
33 placement through the Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services
34 Health and Human Services shall be allowed to remain enrolled in the public
35 school in which the child was enrolled at the time he entered foster care for the
36 duration of the child's stay in the custody of the state or until he completes the
37 highest grade offered at the school if the Louisiana Department of Children and
38 Family Services Health and Human Services determines that remaining in that
39 school is in the best interest of the child. If the foster care placement is outside the
40 jurisdictional boundaries of the public school in which the child is enrolled, the
41 governing authority of such school shall be responsible for providing free
42 transportation for the child to and from a designated location which is within that
43 school district and is located nearest to the child's residence and is determined to be
44 appropriate by such governing authority and the Louisiana Department of Children
45 and Family Services Health and Human Services. The Louisiana Department of
46 Children and Family Services Health and Human Services shall be responsible for
47 providing the child's transportation between that location and the child's residence.
48 * * *

Page 24 of 111

1 permitted under Chapter 1, 4, 5, 7, or 10 of this Title shall pay the remainder to the

3 overpayments. If the remainder is equal to or less than zero, the person who has an
4 outstanding child support arrearage or child support overpayment shall not receive
5 a payment.

33 Section 13. R.S. 28:31, 470(B)(8) and (10), and 621 are hereby amended and
34 reenacted to read as follows:
35 §31. Findings
36 The legislature finds that there is a need for a secured residential facility for
37 any person found not guilty of a crime by reason of insanity or found incompetent
38 to stand trial after such person has been released from a state forensic facility.
39 Historically, all secured residential facilities have been overseen by the Department
40 of Children and Family Services under its authority to regulate traditional adult
41 residential care homes. Nevertheless, it is now more appropriate and efficient for the
42 Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services to license and regulate
43 secured residential facilities serving forensic clients due to the mental health issues
44 of the residents, the fact that the individuals are discharged from forensic hospitals
45 operated by the Louisiana Department of Health, and the security issues involved at
46 such facilities. Thus, the licensing of secured residential facilities serving forensic
47 clients shall be transferred from the Department of Children and Family Services to
48 the Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services and licensed as forensic
49 supervised transitional residential and aftercare facilities in accordance with this Part.
50 The licensing of all other adult residential care homes shall remain in the Department
51 of Children and Family Services pursuant to R.S. 40:2151 through 2161.

53 CHAPTER 6. LOUISIANA DEPARTMENT OF HEALTH AND HUMAN SERVICES
54 §251. Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services; creation; domicile;
55 composition; purpose and functions
56 A. The Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services is created and
57 shall be a body corporate with the power to sue and be sued. The domicile of the
58 department shall be in Baton Rouge where it shall maintain its principal offices, but
59 the secretary may maintain branch offices if he deems it in the best interest of the
60 efficient administration of the department; however, the principal offices of the
61 office of public health may be located and maintained in the parish of Orleans.
Page 27 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 B. The Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services, through its
2 offices and officers, shall be responsible for the development and providing of health
3 and medical services for the prevention of disease for the citizens of Louisiana. The
4 Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services shall provide health and
5 medical services for the uninsured and medically indigent citizens of Louisiana. The
6 secretary and the chancellor of the Louisiana State University Health Sciences
7 Center shall provide for coordination in the delivery of services provided by the
8 Louisiana State University Health Sciences Center with those services provided by
9 the Louisiana Department of Health, local health departments, and federally qualified
10 health centers, including but not limited to the following:
11 (1) Services for any of the following persons:
12 (a) Persons with mental illness.
13 (b) Persons with intellectual disabilities.
14 (c) Persons with developmental disabilities.
15 (d) Persons with addictive disorders.
16 (2) Public health services.
17 (3) Services provided under the medical assistance program (Medicaid).
18 C.(1) The Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services shall be
19 composed of the executive office of the secretary, the office of the surgeon general,
20 the office of management and finance, the office of public health, the office of
21 behavioral health, the office for citizens with developmental disabilities, the office
22 of aging and adult services, the office on women's health and community health, and
23 such other offices as shall be created by law.

46 (cc) Communication and advocacy on the child's behalf with care
47 coordinators.

49 (ee) Twenty-four hour on-call crisis assistance to respond to the needs of
50 the child.
51 (ff) Assistance with transportation and other physical needs.
52 (gg) Support work with the family to develop safety procedures based on
53 the particular situation and the child's needs.
54 (hh) Education on how to monitor and address the child's internet
55 access, messaging, and telephone contacts.

11 §1023. Drug administration course; certification of medication attendants; rules;
12 instructor training courses; fees
13 A. Drug administration courses shall be established by the office of the
14 secretary of the Louisiana Department of Health in conjunction with the Louisiana
15 State Board of Nursing and the Louisiana State Board of Practical Nurse Examiners
16 and as approved by the secretary of the Louisiana Department of Health. Persons
17 who have successfully completed the course and passed a qualifying examination
18 shall be permitted to administer certain medications to residents of facilities operated
19 by the office for citizens with developmental disabilities or community homes for
20 persons with developmental disabilities funded through the Louisiana Department
21 of Health and Human Services or the Department of Children and Family Services
22 and to persons receiving in-home Medicaid home- and community-based services
23 and shall be known as medication attendants. The course shall include but not be
24 limited to instruction of the legal aspects, roles, and responsibilities of drug
25 administration, definitions, terminology, classification, measurement, identification,
26 effects, distribution, and the care and handling of drugs.
27 B. Fees for the drug administration courses shall be determined by the office
28 of the secretary of the Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services. The
29 cost of implementation will be reimbursed to providers with contracts by the
30 Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services or the Department of
31 Children and Family Services.

43 §100.181. Continuum of Care Fund
44 A. There is hereby established in the state treasury as a special fund the
45 Continuum of Care Fund, hereafter referred to in this Section as the "fund". Monies
46 appropriated or transferred to the fund shall be deposited by the state treasurer after
47 compliance with the requirements of Article VII, Section 9(B) of the Constitution of
48 Louisiana relative to the Bond Security and Redemption Fund. Monies in the fund
49 shall be invested in the same manner as monies in the state general fund. Interest
50 earned on investment of monies in the fund shall be credited to the fund. Until
51 December 1, 2024, unexpended and unencumbered monies in the fund at the end of
52 the fiscal year shall remain in the fund. The treasurer is hereby authorized and
53 directed to transfer any unexpended and unencumbered monies in the fund on
54 December 1, 2024, and any interest attributable to such funds, to the Louisiana
55 Rescue Plan Fund. Monies in the fund shall be used by the Louisiana Department
56 of Children and Family Services Health and Human Services to fund continuum
57 of care initiatives.

23 §1086.11. Physician notification
24 A. If a newborn exhibits symptoms of withdrawal or other observable and
25 harmful effects in his physical appearance or functioning that a physician believes
26 are due to the use of a controlled dangerous substance, as defined by R.S. 40:961 et
27 seq., in a lawfully prescribed manner by the mother during pregnancy, the physician
28 shall make a notification to the Louisiana Department of Children and Family
29 Services Health and Human Services on a form developed by the department. Such
30 notification shall not constitute a report of child abuse or prenatal neglect, nor shall
31 it require prosecution for any illegal action.
32 B. A healthcare provider shall be authorized to share any protected health
33 information, as defined in 45 CFR 160.103, with the Louisiana Department of
34 Children and Family Services Health and Human Services for the purpose of
35 complying with the notification requirement of this Subpart.
36 C. The Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services Health and
37 Human Services shall promulgate rules and regulations in accordance with the
38 Administrative Procedure Act to implement the provisions of this Subpart. Such
39 rules shall include, at minimum, all of the following:
40 (1) The manner in which the notification shall be made to the department.
41 (2) The form and minimum required contents of the notification.
42 (3) The plan to monitor the statewide system regarding the availability and
43 delivery of appropriate services for newborns and affected families and caretakers.
44 D. A physician who in good faith makes a notification to the Louisiana
45 Department of Children and Family Services Health and Human Services in
46 compliance with this Section shall have no civil or criminal liability for damage or
47 injury arising from that notification, unless the damage or injury was caused by the
48 physician's willful or wanton misconduct or gross negligence.

39 * * *
40 §52.1. Integrated case management; service integration of various social service
41 programs
42 A. The legislature recognizes that the Louisiana Department of Health and
43 Human Services, Department of Children and Family Services, and Louisiana
44 Works provide services to individuals with multiple needs. However, the
45 conventional service delivery system of requiring individuals to access various
46 offices within the state to address those multiple needs creates barriers to the delivery
47 of those services and entry into the workforce. These needs can be better met, more
48 efficiently and less costly, through integrated case management at a single service
49 location with a single case worker. It is the intent of the legislature to streamline the
50 delivery of services and incorporate integrated case management models for clients
51 and families served by multiple departments and programs.
52 * * *
53 §54. Parish offices
54 A. There shall be in each parish of the state a parish office of the department;
55 provided that the department may unite two or more parishes and form a district
56 office. All duties and responsibilities set forth in this Chapter for parish offices shall
57 also apply to the district offices.
58 B. Under rules and regulations of the department, the field and district
59 offices shall administer all forms of public assistance within the department's
60 purview in respective parishes.
61 * * *

1 §56. Applications and client case records; definitions; confidentiality; waiver;

3 A. Applications for assistance and information contained in case records of

18 elderly affairs share access to each other's case records to the extent that such access
19 is not prohibited by any contrary provision of federal law or regulation.

11 §107. Appeal and review; venue for judicial review
12 A.(1) The Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana Works
13 and the office of the secretary of the Louisiana Department of Health, through their
14 respective appeal sections, shall provide for a system of hearings and are responsible
15 for fulfillment of all hearing provisions as prescribed under Title I, IV-A, X, XIV,
16 XVI, XIX, or XX of the Social Security Act and under the Food Stamp Act, Public
17 Law 91-671. Under these provisions, an opportunity for a hearing shall be granted
18 at the state level to any applicant, or recipient, or customer who makes a timely
19 request for a hearing because his claim for assistance, services, or nutrition
20 assistance benefits is denied or is not acted upon with reasonable promptness and to
21 any recipient who is aggrieved by an agency action resulting in suspension,
22 reduction, discontinuance, or termination of benefits.
23 (2) Under these provisions, an opportunity for a hearing shall also be granted
24 at the state level by the Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services
25 Health and Human Services to any child placing agency or day care center who is
26 aggrieved by any agency action resulting in the denial, suspension, or revocation of
27 a license.
28 * * *
29 E. For purposes of this Section, "customer" means an applicant or
30 recipient of public assistance benefits and services that fall within the purview
31 of Louisiana Works.
32 * * *
33 §114. Fraud in obtaining assistance; withholding information concerning property,
34 income or beneficiary, or personal circumstances
35 A. No person shall obtain or attempt to obtain assistance from the
36 Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana Works or the Louisiana
37 Department of Health and Human Services by means of any false statement,
38 misrepresentation, or other fraudulent device. If during the life, or upon the death,
39 of any person who is receiving or has received assistance it is found that the recipient
40 is receiving or has received assistance through misrepresentation, nondisclosure of
41 material facts, or other fraudulent device, the amount of assistance, without interest,
42 shall be recoverable from him or his estate as a debt due the state by court action.
43 B. If at any time during the continuance of public assistance to any person,
44 the recipient thereof, or the husband or wife of the recipient with whom he or she is
45 living, is possessed or becomes possessed of any property or income in excess of the
46 amount declared at the time of application or reinvestigation of his case and in such
47 amount as would affect his needs or right to receive assistance, it shall be the duty
48 of the recipient, or the husband or wife of the recipient, to notify the Department of
49 Children and Family Services Louisiana Works or the Louisiana Department of
50 Health and Human Services of possession of such property or income, and the
51 department shall, after investigation, either cancel the assistance or alter the amount
52 thereof in accordance with the circumstances, provided, that such investigation
53 shows that such property or income does affect the need of the recipient or his right
54 to receive assistance. If during the life, or upon the death, of any person who is
55 receiving or has received assistance it is found that the recipient or his spouse was
56 possessed of any property or income in excess of the amount reported that would
57 affect his need or right to receive assistance, any assistance paid when the recipient
58 or his spouse was in possession of such undeclared property or income shall be
59 recoverable, without interest, from him or his estate as a debt due the state by court
60 action. The possession of undeclared property by a recipient or his spouse with
61 whom he is living shall be prima facie evidence of its ownership during the time
Page 40 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 assistance was granted, and the burden to prove otherwise shall be upon the recipient
2 or his legal representative.
3 C.(1) If the personal circumstances of the recipient change at any time during
4 the continuance of assistance, he shall immediately notify the Department of
5 Children and Family Services Louisiana Works or the Louisiana Department of
6 Health and Human Services of the change. Personal circumstances shall include:
7 * * *
8 (2) If during the life, or upon the death, of any person who is receiving
9 assistance it is found that the recipient has received or is receiving assistance of a
10 greater amount than he is entitled to receive as a result of his failure to notify the
11 Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana Works or the Louisiana
12 Department of Health and Human Services of a change of personal circumstances
13 as set forth in this Subsection, any assistance paid during the time that the recipient
14 was receiving assistance of a greater amount than he was entitled to receive as a
15 result of his failure to notify the department shall be recoverable, with legal interest,
16 from him or his estate as a debt due the state by court action.
17 D. The federal government shall be entitled to share in any amount recovered
18 under the provisions of this Section; however, the amount recovered by the federal
19 government shall not exceed the amount contributed by the federal government in
20 each case. The amount due the United States shall be promptly paid or credited upon
21 collection to the designated agency of the federal government by the Department of
22 Children and Family Services Louisiana Works or the Louisiana Department of
23 Health and Human Services.
24 E.(1) Persons receiving food stamps or Aid to Families with Dependent
25 Children, or a successor of either program, who have been determined by the
26 Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana Works or the Louisiana
27 Department of Health and Human Services in an administrative hearing, or a
28 court of competent jurisdiction after final appeal, to have fraudulently obtained such
29 food stamps or Aid to Families with Dependent Children, or benefits or assistance
30 from a successor of either program, shall be ineligible for further participation in the
31 program in accordance with the following schedule:

33 §114.2. Attempting or aiding to obtain assistance fraudulently; penalties
34 Any person who obtains or attempts to obtain or aids and abets anyone to
35 obtain assistance from the Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana
36 Works or the Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services by means of
37 any false statement, misrepresentation, or other fraudulent device or violates the
38 provisions of R.S. 46:114 shall be guilty of theft as provided by R.S. 14:67.
39 §114.3. Regional fraud detection units; investigative subpoenas and subpoenas
40 duces tecum
41 A. The Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana Works shall
42 establish, maintain, and provide for fraud detection functions in order to detect fraud
43 in obtaining public assistance through staff in each region of the state. Each fraud
44 detection unit shall report each incident of public assistance fraud to the fraud
45 detection section of the office of children and family services on a monthly basis by
46 the tenth day of each succeeding month. An annual report of the activities of all fraud
47 detection units within a state fiscal year shall be submitted by the fraud detection
48 section to the Senate and House committees on health and welfare by September
49 first.
50 B. When the secretary of the Department of Children and Family Services
51 Louisiana Works or the secretary's designated representative has evidence that any
52 person, business, or other legal entity attempted to obtain or obtained assistance or
53 payment for services or goods from the department by means of any false statement,
54 misrepresentation, or other fraudulent device, the secretary or the designated
55 representative may issue an administrative investigation subpoena for deposition
56 testimony or a subpoena duces tecum to be served upon any person, business, or
57 other legal entity who is believed to have information, material, or physical evidence
58 relative to the alleged or suspected violation, for the purpose of producing, revealing,
59 identifying, or explaining documentary material or other physical evidence. Such
60 deposition or return of subpoena shall take place in the parish in which the person,
61 business, or other legal entity upon whom the subpoena has been served resides or
62 conducts business. The subpoena shall be served by certified mail, return receipt
Page 41 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 requested, or by any other means authorized by the Code of Civil Procedure or the
2 Code of Criminal Procedure for the service of process. The subpoena shall specify
3 a return date indicating the date by which deposition testimony or information,
4 material, or physical evidence must be received by the department.

6 §116. Prima facie proof of pleadings
7 Pleadings filed on behalf of the Department of Children and Family Services
8 Louisiana Works or the Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services in
9 actions to recover the value of ineligible public financial assistance payments or
10 benefits shall be accompanied by an itemized statement of the amount of
11 overissuance or overpayment together with the amount to which the recipient was
12 entitled, if any. When accompanied by an affidavit of the assistant secretary of the
13 office administering such payments or benefits to the correctness thereof as to the
14 truth of the facts alleged to the best of the affiant's knowledge and belief, such
15 itemized statement shall be accepted as prima facie proof of the disbursement and
16 receipt of said payments and the amount thereof.

26 §230.1. Legislative intent
27 A. It is the intent of the legislature that families in Louisiana be strong and
28 economically self-reliant so as to minimize their dependence on government benefits
29 for basic needs. To accomplish this goal, it is the intent of this Part that the
30 Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana Works ensures that all cash
31 assistance recipients, with the exception of persons with disabilities or who are
32 incapacitated, are actively and universally engaged in meaningful activities designed
33 to enable their transition from cash assistance to self-reliance. It is the further intent
34 that cash assistance participants demonstrate and are expected to exercise active and
35 diligent personal responsibility in achieving self-reliance through employment and
36 increased workplace literacy. All appropriate state agencies responsible for
37 employment, training, and educating Louisiana's citizens are expected to cooperate
38 in the pursuit of this goal.
39 B. The Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana Works shall
40 submit written reports on the status of implementation of these provisions to the
41 Performance Review Subcommittee of the Joint Legislative Committee on the
42 Budget in March, 2004 and September, 2004, and thereafter, annually at the same
43 time as the mid-year performance progress report is submitted as provided in R.S.
44 39:87.3(A)(2). Such written reports shall include but not be limited to data providing
45 performance measures assessing the success of performance-based agreements, job
46 readiness, workplace literacy, job development services, and such additional data as
47 may be determined by the committee.

7 §236.6. Failure to pay support; procedure, penalties and publication
8 A.(1) If a defendant violates the terms of a court order, issued pursuant to the
9 provisions of R.S. 46:236.1.1 et seq. and 236.2, Children's Code Article 1301.1 et
10 seq., or R.S. 13:4241, requiring him to pay child support to the Department of
11 Children and Family Services Justice, a representative of the child support collection
12 agency as set forth in R.S. 46:236.1.8 may issue and serve on the defendant a
13 summons ordering him to appear and show cause before the proper court of
14 competent jurisdiction, on a date which shall be specified by the court, why he
15 should not be held in contempt of court. Prior to or at the hearing, the Department
16 of Children and Family Services Justice or the district attorney shall file with the
17 court any summons served and a rule for contempt which shall be served in open
18 court on the defendant, setting forth the terms of the original court order for child
19 support and all modifications thereof, along with the allegations purporting to place
20 the defendant in contempt. If the defendant denies the allegations or offers a defense
21 to the rule, the court may, upon motion of either party or on its own motion, continue
22 the hearing.
23 * * *
24 C. In addition to any other penalty provided for in this Section, the court shall
25 render judgment in favor of the applicable payee for the amount of unpaid support
26 plus attendant court costs. The judgment shall have the same force and effect as a
27 final judgment for money damages against the defendant. This judgment shall
28 become executory upon its rendition, subject to the delays for filing a motion for new
29 trial or appeal, and may be registered with any Louisiana court of competent
30 jurisdiction on petition of the Department of Children and Family Services Justice,
31 the district attorney's office, or the applicable payee.
32 * * *
33 E. The termination of a court order issued pursuant to the provisions of R.S.
34 46:236.1.1 et seq. and 236.2, Children's Code Article 1301.1 et seq., or R.S. 13:4241,
35 requiring a defendant to pay child support to the Department of Children and Family
36 Services Justice does not abate the power of any court or the department to collect
37 any overdue and unpaid support or arrearage owed under the terminated support
38 order or the power of the court to punish any person for a failure to comply with, or
39 to pay any support as ordered in, the terminated court order.
40 * * *
41 G.(1) Upon request of any representative of a newspaper and to the extent
42 permitted by federal law, the Department of Children and Family Services Justice
43 shall supply a list of names and addresses of all persons who have been found guilty
44 of criminal neglect of family as provided in R.S. 14:74 et seq. or who have been
45 found in contempt of court for failure to comply with a support order enforced by the
46 Department of Children and Family Services Justice. The newspaper may publish
47 such a list or any part of this list it considers necessary.
48 (2) The Department of Children and Family Services Justice may adopt rules
49 governing the publication of the names of persons who are delinquent in the payment
50 of child support obligations under orders which are enforced by the department and
51 the publication of information which is related to those delinquent payments. The
52 rules shall be adopted in accordance with the Administrative Procedure Act and shall
53 establish the criteria for the selection of the individuals whose names may be
54 published, the criteria for the determination of the types and amount of related
55 information which may be published, and the criteria for the determination of the
56 types of media and individual media outlets in which the names and related
57 information may be published. The department may publish the names and related
58 information at the expense of the department or may release the names and related
59 information for publication on a public service basis.
60 * * *

38 §236.8. Medical support orders; health insurance enforcement
39 A. When a court orders a parent to provide medical support for the child,
40 specifically requiring the parent to enroll or maintain the child in a health insurance
41 program, the Department of Children and Family Services Justice, in any case in
42 which the department is rendering services, shall enforce the court order through the
43 use of the National Medical Support Notice, regarding group health plans that are
44 covered under the provisions of 42 U.S.C. §666(a)(19), 29 U.S.C. §1169, and 45
45 CFR §303.32, and shall serve on the parent's employer the National Medical Support
46 Notice to enroll the child and employee in the employee's health insurance program
47 in accordance with the medical support order.
48 * * *
49 G. When a court orders a parent who is a participant or is eligible to
50 participate in a group health plan to enroll or maintain a minor child in a health
51 insurance program, the insurance company or health maintenance organization shall:
52 * * *
53 (5) Allow the provider, or the Louisiana Department of Health and Human
54 Services for the Medicaid Plan, or the Department of Children and Family Services
55 to submit claims for covered services without the approval of the custodial or the
56 noncustodial parent.
57 (6) Reimburse the parent who rendered payment for services for the child, the
58 provider, or the Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services for the
59 Medicaid Plan, or the Department of Children and Family Services directly for
60 claims submitted by them.

62 §236.9. Collection of child support; cooperative program
Page 48 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 * * *
2 B. When a delinquency is referred to the Department of Revenue, hereinafter
3 referred to in this Section as the "department", pursuant to the provisions of this
4 Section, the amount of child support due, and any accrued interest and costs shall be
5 collected from the obligated parent by the department in any manner authorized by
6 law, and as specifically provided in Part III of Chapter 18 of Subtitle II of Title 47
7 of the Louisiana Revised Statutes. All funds generated from the collection efforts
8 shall be remitted periodically to the Department of Children and Family Services
9 Justice for distribution as provided by law for collected child support payments.
10 However, the department shall be entitled to any allowable federal reimbursement,
11 and to fifty percent of any fees or payments that would ordinarily be due to the
12 Department of Children and Family Services Justice for the collection made, except
13 for incentives.
14 * * *
15 G. In the event the collection action would cause undue hardship to the
16 obligated parent, would threaten the health or welfare of his family, or would cause
17 irreparable loss, the obligated parent may so notify the secretary. In such case, the
18 secretary may, in his discretion, refer the receipt of such information to the secretary
19 of the Department of Children and Family Services Justice, who shall determine
20 whether to halt the department's collection procedures.
21 * * *
22 K. The Department of Revenue and the Department of Children and Family

14 §236.16. Child support mortgage and privilege by affidavit; effect of filing
15 A. The director of the child support enforcement section, office of children
16 and family services Department of Children and Family Services division of the
17 Department of Justice may cause a "Child Support Mortgage and Privilege by
18 Affidavit of DCFS", as provided in R.S. 13:4291(B), to be recorded in the mortgage
19 records of any parish in which the support obligor owns movable or immovable
20 property, and with the office of the secretary of state for inclusion in the master
21 index authorized under R.S. 10:9-519. Such affidavit when filed shall operate as a
22 first lien, privilege, and legal mortgage on all of the movable and immovable
23 property of the support obligor only from the date of such filing, and shall not affect
24 liens, privileges, chattel mortgages, or security interests as provided in R.S. 10:9-101
25 et seq. or mortgages already affecting or burdening such property at the date of such
26 filing. Such filing shall apply to all unpaid support obligations that may accrue after
27 such filing, and the property of the support obligor shall be subject to seizure and
28 sale for the payment of such support obligation and arrearages according to the
29 preference and rank of the lien, privilege, security interest, and mortgage securing
30 their payment. Notwithstanding any provision of this Subsection, such affidavit shall
31 not operate as a lien, privilege, or legal mortgage on any licensed or titled motor
32 vehicle.
33 B. The director of the child support enforcement section, office of children
34 and family services, Department of Children and Family Services division of the
35 Department of Justice, or his designee, may release all or any portion of the
36 property subject to any lien or judgment obtained pursuant to this Section from such
37 lien or judgment, or may subordinate such lien or judgment to other liens and
38 encumbrances if he determines that the support obligation and arrearages are
39 sufficiently secured by a lien or judgment on other property or through other
40 security, or that the release, partial release, or subordination of such lien or judgment
41 will not endanger or jeopardize the collection of support obligations or arrearages.
42 * * *

56 §282. Investigation of foster and adoptive parent applicants
57 A. The Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services Health and
58 Human Services, office of children and family services child welfare, shall
59 investigate the background of each person who applies to be a foster or adoptive
60 parent of a child in foster care. The investigation required by this Section shall
61 include but shall not be limited to a determination of whether the applicant or any
62 adult member of the applicant's household has been charged with a crime and, if so,
Page 52 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 the disposition of those charges. The office shall require each applicant and adult
2 family member to provide fingerprints and such authorization as is necessary to
3 conduct state and national criminal history record checks and to obtain any other
4 information required to complete the investigation. The department is authorized to
5 promulgate regulations as may be necessary to conduct the criminal history record
6 checks authorized in this Section.
7 B. The office of children and family services child welfare shall request such
8 information and assistance from federal, state, or local governmental agencies as is
9 necessary to complete the investigation required by this Section. Only information
10 which bears a reasonable relation to the performance of the duties of a foster parent
11 shall be requested.
12 C. The office of children and family services child welfare shall not require
13 an applicant to provide any physical identity materials other than photographs or
14 fingerprints. Such materials shall be returned to the applicant upon completion of the
15 investigation, and no copy of such materials may be retained by the office or by any
16 agency to which such identity materials were transmitted.
17 * * *

40 and Family Services Health and Human Services shall, at the initial time of contact

43 manner that is consistent with laws protecting the rights of the informant.

45 Council on Social Work Education accredited program of social work certifying that

47 areas of effective child welfare practice, including successful completion of a child

16 §286. Foster home child care; reimbursement system; rules
17 The Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services Health and
18 Human Services shall establish a system for reimbursement of foster home child
19 care costs based on the level of care for all foster children placed in foster homes
20 providing temporary or long-term foster care for not more than six children receiving
21 the services of the department. The department shall promulgate rules for
22 implementation of the reimbursement system by January 1, 1995, but only if funds
23 are made available by appropriation by the legislature, and shall submit such rules
24 to the committees on health and welfare of the House of Representatives and the
25 Senate in accordance with the Administrative Procedure Act. At a minimum, the
26 department shall seek each year through the budgetary process funds sufficient to
27 reimburse foster parents at a rate at least equal to the cost for child care as reported
28 and published by the United States Department of Agriculture for the Southeastern
29 United States.
30 §286.1. Kinship Foster Care Program
31 A. As used in this Section the following terms shall have the following
32 meaning:
33 (1) "Department" means the Louisiana Department of Children and Family
34 Services Health and Human Services.
35 (2) "Foster parent" means any person with whom a child in the care, custody,
36 or guardianship of the office of children and family services Louisiana Department
37 of Health and Human Services is placed for temporary or long-term care of not
38 more than three years, but shall not include any person with whom a child is placed
39 for the purpose of adoption.
40 (3) "Office" means the office of children and family services child welfare
41 of the Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services Health and Human
42 Services.
43 B. There is hereby established a Kinship Foster Care Program in the office
44 of children and family services child welfare of the Louisiana Department of
45 Children and Family Services Health and Human Services.
46 C.(1) Except as provided by Paragraph (2) of this Subsection, when a child
47 has been removed from his home and is in the care, custody, or guardianship of the
48 office of children and family services child welfare, the office shall make reasonable
49 attempts to place the child with a relative for kinship foster care. If the relative is
50 approved by the office to provide foster care services, in accordance with rules and
51 regulations adopted by the Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services
52 Health and Human Services regarding foster care services and a placement with
53 the relative is made, the relative shall be eligible to receive payment for the full
54 foster care rate for the care of the child and any other benefits that might be available
55 to foster parents, whether in money or in service. The reimbursement rate shall be
56 in accordance with the system established by the department pursuant to R.S. 46:286.
57 * * *
58 (3) A relative may continue to be eligible for foster care reimbursement for
59 caring for a child in the care, custody, or guardianship of the office of children and
60 family services beyond three years when:

54 §286.12. Purpose
55 Foster parents are recognized as primary care givers to abused and neglected
56 children who have been removed from their homes of origin. The Louisiana
57 Department of Children and Family Services Health and Human Services shall
58 implement and promote the support of these rights through the policy and practice
59 of the Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services Health and Human
60 Services.

41 §401. Reciprocal agreements regarding interstate transportation of poor and indigent
42 The Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services Health and
43 Human Services, subject to the approval of the attorney general, may enter into
44 reciprocal agreements with corresponding state agencies of other states regarding the
45 interstate transportation of poor and indigent persons, and may arrange with the
46 proper officials in this state for the acceptance, transfer, and support of persons
47 receiving public aid in other states in accordance with the terms of the reciprocal
48 agreements; provided that this state shall not, nor shall any parish or other political
49 subdivision of this state, be committed to the support of persons who are not, in the
50 opinion of the department, entitled to public support by the laws of this state.
51 * * *
52 §441. Surviving spouse of public assistance recipients; retention of benefits received
53 during month of death
54 A surviving spouse of a general public assistance recipient is hereby
55 authorized to receive and retain any financial assistance paid by the Department of
56 Children and Family Services Louisiana Works to or for the benefit of said the
57 recipient during the month of the death of said recipient, whether or not the check
58 covering such the public assistance was actually received prior to the death of the
59 recipient.

17 §447. Revision of standard of need; aid to families with dependent children; general
18 assistance
19 A. The Louisiana Department of Health and the Department of Children and
20 Family Services Louisiana Works jointly shall revise the standard of need for the
21 Family Independence Temporary Assistanct Assistance Program and the general
22 assistance program each year, basing such standard on the Annual Update of the
23 Poverty Income Guidelines published by the United States Department of Health and
24 Human Services. The standard shall reflect the higher of the southern and national
25 averages. The departments shall cause such revised standard to become effective on
26 January first of each year.
27 B. Implementation of this provision shall be contingent on the Louisiana
28 Department of Health and Human Services and the Department of Children and
29 Family Services Louisiana Works certifying to the commissioner of the division of
30 administration that the revision will not increase the total state dollar expenditure for
31 the two departments.
32 * * *
33 §447.3. In-hospital mental health care for adopted children; state's duty to furnish
34 To the extent funds are appropriated by the legislature for such purpose, in
35 all adoption subsidy agreements executed after September 1, 2001, involving a child
36 in the custody of the Louisiana Department of Children and Family Services Health
37 and Human Services, the state shall agree to provide acutely medically necessary
38 in-hospital mental health treatment for that child until he reaches the age of majority,
39 provided that the child is not eligible for, or has otherwise exhausted benefits under
40 Medicaid, LaCHIP, or any contract of health and accident insurance or any health
41 benefit plan. The burden of providing the appropriate documentation of the child's
42 eligibility for medical benefits under this statute shall be upon the adoptive parents.
43 * * *
44 §448. Emergency assistance information and referral
45 A. As used in this Section:
46 (1) "Office of children and family services" shall mean the office of children
47 and family services, Department of Children and Family Services, state of Louisiana.
48 (2)(1) "Emergency assistance" shall mean any service, food, clothing, shelter,
49 money grant, or any other assistance available to people who find their ability to
50 obtain the necessities of life threatened by fire, flood, death, or other sudden and
51 necessitous circumstances.
52 (3)(2) "Governmental agency" shall mean any political subdivision
53 department, office, agency, board, corporation, or other instrumentality funded in
54 whole or in part by local, state, or federal funds that provides some form of
55 emergency assistance in this state.
56 (4)(3) "Private agency" shall mean any department, office, agency, board,
57 corporation, or other instrumentality that provides some form of emergency
58 assistance in this state, but shall not include any private agency that chooses not to
59 take referrals or discriminates in their assistance on the grounds of race.
60 B. The office of children and family services Louisiana Department of
61 Health and Human Services shall gather through its local offices information on
62 all governmental and private agencies in each parish as to the type of assistance each
Page 57 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 agency can and will provide and as to what eligibility requirements, if any, these
2 agencies apply to their assistance.
3 C. The office of children and family services Louisiana Department of
4 Health and Human Services shall designate an office in each parish which will aid
5 people seeking emergency assistance, either in person or by telephone, to identify
6 what assistance, if any, the person can obtain. The office of children and family
7 services shall publicize in each parish the availability of this information.
8 D. Each office will report at the end of each calendar year to the assistant
9 secretary of the office of children and family services Louisiana Department of
10 Health and Human Services, the total number and type of emergency assistance
11 requests it has received and the number and type of emergency assistance requests
12 for which no agency provides assistance in that area. The reports shall be available
13 to the public on request.
14 E. The services provided pursuant to this Section shall be funded from such
15 monies as are already provided for the office of children and family services
16 Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services, and to this end, shall be
17 deemed not to require additional personnel or appropriations.

48 §460.5. Earned income disregards for certain TANF recipients
49 A. In order to promote self-sufficiency, the Department of Children and
50 Family Services Louisiana Works shall disregard a recipient's first six months of
51 earnings up to nine hundred dollars of gross earnings per month in determining the
52 amount of his household's benefit under Temporary Assistance for Needy Families,
53 provided that such the recipient is engaged in a work activity which has been
54 approved by the department as part of his work participation requirement under
55 TANF.
56 * * *
57 §460.7. Incentive Award Program; dropout reduction; teen pregnancy reduction
58 A. The Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana Works in
59 consultation with the Department of Education shall develop and implement a
60 special program, the Incentive Award Program, whereby the governing authority of
61 a parish and a parish school system may receive a financial award for reducing the
62 teen pregnancy rate and dropout rate for the parish.
Page 58 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 * * *
2 C. Through the Incentive Award Program, the department shall provide a
3 financial award to each of the ten parishes identified in the annual progress report
4 which that have demonstrated the most significant reduction in dropout rates, as
5 defined by rule of the Department of Education, and in teen pregnancy rates as
6 defined by rule of the Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana
7 Works. The financial award shall be distributed to such the ten parish school
8 systems. These awards may be expended by the parish school system to implement
9 innovative community-based and school-based programs designed to further reduce
10 the dropout rate and the teen pregnancy rate for the parish and for instructional
11 enhancement programs.
12 * * *
13 §460.8. TANF eligibility; teen parent living arrangements; work participation
14 requirements; submission of waiver
15 A.(1)(a) Any recipient of Temporary Assistance for Needy Families Block
16 Grant (TANF) benefits who is less than eighteen years of age, is not married, and is
17 a custodial parent shall live in an approved adult-supervised living arrangement with
18 his or her child, except when evidence is presented to a caseworker of the
19 Department of Children and Family Services Louisiana Works that the teen parent,
20 or his or her child, has been subjected to emotional or physical abuse.
21 (b)(i) If the caseworker determines that the teen parent, or his or her child,
22 has been subjected to the abuse of an adult with whom they are living in a primary
23 relationship and that under the circumstances the teen, and his or her child, would be
24 safer living outside the present adult-supervised living arrangement, then the teen
25 parent and child shall be allowed to live outside such the adult-supervised living
26 arrangement temporarily.
27 (ii) If the teen parent leaves his or her such the adult-supervised living
28 arrangement, the caseworker shall monitor the teen's case no less frequently than
29 once a month and shall assist the teen parent in locating another approved adult-
30 supervised living arrangement, taking into consideration the needs and concerns of
31 the teen parent and child.
32 (c) The teen parent shall be allowed to receive TANF benefits on behalf of
33 himself or herself, and his or her child, while temporarily living outside an adult-
34 supervised living arrangement as provided in this Subsection.
35 * * *
36 B. The secretary of the Department of Children and Family Services
37 Louisiana Works may temporarily exempt from the work participation requirements
38 any female who is in a two-parent TANF family who presents sufficient evidence to
39 support a claim that she has been incapable of maintaining a job or regularly
40 reporting to her place of employment because she is a victim of domestic violence
41 and has been forced to move into a shelter or another protective environment outside
42 her home.
43 * * *
44 §460.10. Drug testing for certain adult recipients of public assistance; legislative
45 policy; procedures
46 A. The legislature hereby reaffirms the legitimate government function of
47 promoting the safety and welfare of children and adults. The legislature declares that
48 the best interests of a significant portion of the state's population are served by
49 ensuring that they are free of the physical and mental impairments associated with
50 drug dependence. The legislature further reaffirms its compelling interest in
51 providing safeguards to eliminate the misappropriation of entitlement public
52 assistance benefits. The legislature hereby directs the secretary of the Department
53 of Children and Family Services Louisiana Works, in consultation with the
54 secretary of the Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services and the
55 commissioner of administration, to establish a mandatory drug testing program for
56 certain adults in the Temporary Assistance for Needy Families Block Grant Program.
57 B.(1) The secretary of the Department of Children and Family Services
58 Louisiana Works shall cause to be instituted a mandatory drug testing program for
59 certain adult participants, to be determined by the secretary in consultation with the
60 secretary of the Louisiana Department of Health and Human Services and the
61 commissioner of administration, in the Temporary Assistance for Needy Families
62 Block Grant Program. However, no No participant shall be tested if such testing is
Page 59 of 111

SCASB462 3005 1692
1 prohibited by federal law. No sanction shall be imposed on an adult participant if
2 such sanction is prohibited by federal law.
3 (2) The Such testing program shall provide procedural safeguards to ensure
4 the protection of the constitutional rights of the program participants and provide that
5 testing shall be done by state certified laboratories.
6 C.(1) The required drug testing program shall require a participant to
7 complete an education and rehabilitation program upon the initial identification of
8 such the participant as an illegal drug user verified by a positive test result as a
9 prerequisite to continued receipt of benefits. Further, the drug testing program shall
10 provide for the suspension of participation in such entitlement the public assistance
11 program for a participant subsequently identified by a verified positive test result as
12 an illegal drug user; however. However, in no event shall participation in such
13 entitlement the public assistance program be suspended while the participant is
14 taking part in the education and rehabilitation program or until an education and
15 rehabilitation program is available to the participant.
16 (2)(a) The secretary of the Department of Children and Family Services
17 Louisiana Works, in conjunction with the secretary of the Louisiana Department of
18 Health and Human Services and the commissioner of administration, shall provide
19 a program of education and rehabilitation for participants so identified as illegal drug
20 users.
21 (b) Such The program shall include regulations governing the reentry of a
22 suspended recipient participant into the entitlement public assistance program
23 based on subsequent testing results and completion of education and rehabilitation
24 programs.
25 (c) Such The program shall also include the provision of inpatient services
26 for any participant identified as an illegal drug user if it is determined that such
27 inpatient services are necessary for successful rehabilitation.
28 D. The secretary of the Department of Children and Family Services
29 Louisiana Works, in consultation with the secretary of the Louisiana Department
30 of Health and Human Services and the commissioner of administration, shall
31 promulgate rules and regulations to implement the provisions of this Section in
32 accordance with the Administrative Procedure Act. Such rules and regulations shall
33 provide that the cost of testing participants for the presence of illegal drugs and the
34 treatment of such participants pursuant to the provisions of this Section shall be
35 borne by the department or departments that grant the applicable public assistance.
36 E. The secretary of Louisiana Works shall prepare a written statistical report
37 on the program and submit the report to the legislature on or before January 1, 1999
38 and annually thereafter.

45 * * *

49 provided seventy-two hours of safe harbor unless otherwise designated by order of
50 a court exercising juvenile jurisdiction regarding custody of the runaway youth, or

56 to provide care for the runaway youth pending a determination by the Louisiana
57 Department of Children and Family Services Health and Human Services or a
58 court exercising juvenile jurisdiction regarding custody of the runaway youth.
